node -e "const mongoose = require('mongoose'); const URI = 'mongodb+srv://dwaithdevkalyan_db_user:2TfgyQfGmpiuImO9@monkeysurvey.jufdxfk.mongodb.net/monkeysurvey?appName=monkeysurvey'; async function run() { await mongoose.connect(URI); const coll = mongoose.connection.collection('msr_responses'); const targetSurveyId = '6997e719071aea1670643e21'; const responses = await coll.find({ surveyId: targetSurveyId }).toArray(); console.log('Found ' + responses.length + ' responses to update'); for (const r of responses) { if (!r.answers || !r.answers.length) continue; const toStr = (v) => Array.isArray(v) ? (v[0] || '') : (v || ''); const updates = {}; updates.parliament = toStr(r.answers[0]?.value); updates.municipality = toStr(r.answers[1]?.value); updates.ward_num = toStr(r.answers[2]?.value); updates.village_or_street = toStr(r.answers[3]?.value); updates.assembly = updates.municipality; updates.mandal = updates.ward_num; r.answers.forEach((ans, index) => { updates['Question_' + (index + 1)] = ans.value; }); const phoneAns = r.answers[6]?.value; if (phoneAns) { updates.userName = phoneAns; } await coll.updateOne({ _id: r._id }, { $set: updates }); } console.log('Migration complete'); process.exit(0); } run();"

(v[0] || '') : (v || ''); const updates = {}; updates.parliament = toStr(r.answers[0]?.value); updates.municipality = toStr(r.answers[1]?.value); updates.ward_num = toStr(r.answers[2]?.value); updates.village_or_street = toStr(r.answers[3]?.value); updates.assembly = updates.municipality; updates.mandal = updates.ward_num; r.answers.forEach((ans, index) => { updates['Question_' + (index + 1)] = ans.value; }); const phoneAns = r.answers[6]?.value; if (phoneAns) { updates.userName = phoneAns; } await coll.updateOne({ _id: r._id }, { $set: updates }); } console.log('Migration complete'); } catch (err) { console.error('Error:', err); } finally { await mongoose.disconnect(); process.exit(0); } } run();"

(v[0] || '') : (v || ''); const updates = {}; updates.parliament = toStr(r.answers[0]?.value); updates.municipality = toStr(r.answers[1]?.value); updates.ward_num = toStr(r.answers[2]?.value); updates.village_or_street = toStr(r.answers[3]?.value); updates.assembly = updates.municipality; updates.mandal = updates.ward_num; r.answers.forEach((ans, index) => { updates['Question_' + (index + 1)] = ans.value; }); const phoneAns = r.answers[6]?.value; if (phoneAns) { updates.userName = phoneAns; } await coll.updateOne({ _id: r._id }, { $set: updates }); count++; if (count % 10 === 0) console.log('Updated ' + count + ' responses'); } console.log('Migration complete. (v[0] || '') : (v || ''); for (const r of responses) { if (!r.answers || !r.answers.length) continue; const updates = {}; updates.parliament = toStr(r.answers[0]?.value); updates.municipality = toStr(r.answers[1]?.value); updates.ward_num = toStr(r.answers[2]?.value); updates.village_or_street = toStr(r.answers[3]?.value); updates.assembly = updates.municipality; updates.mandal = updates.ward_num; r.answers.forEach((ans, index) => { updates['Question_' + (index + 1)] = ans.value; }); const phoneAns = r.answers[6]?.value; if (phoneAns) { updates.userName = phoneAns; } await coll.updateOne({ _id: r._id }, { $set: updates }); count++; if (count % 5 === 0) console.log('Updated ' + count + ' records...'); } console.log('COMPLETED: ' + count + ' records updated'); } catch (err) { console.error('ERROR:', err); } finally { await mongoose.disconnect(); process.exit(0); } } run();"
